[7m Manual page ssh-agent(1) line 6 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K[m
[7m Manual page ssh-agent(1) line 7 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       [1m-a [4m[22mbind_address[0m[m
[7m Manual page ssh-agent(1) line 8 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K               Bind  the  agent  to  the  Unix-domain  socket[m
[7m Manual page ssh-agent(1) line 9 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K               [4mbind_address[24m.       The       default       is[m
[7m Manual page ssh-agent(1) line 10 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K               [4m$TMPDIR/ssh-XXXXXXXXXX/agent.<ppid>[24m.[m
[7m Manual page ssh-agent(1) line 11 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K[m
[7m Manual page ssh-agent(1) line 12 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K       [1m-c      [22mGenerate  C-shell commands on stdout.  This is[m
[7m Manual page ssh-agent(1) line 13 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K               the default if SHELL looks  like  it's  a  csh[m
[7m Manual page ssh-agent(1) line 14 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K [KESCESC[KOO[KBB[K               style of shell.[m
[7m Manual page ssh-agent(1) line 15 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K[7mCannot edit standard input  (press RETURN)[27m[18;1H[K[K[7m Manual page ssh-agent(1) line 15 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K[m
       [1m-D      [22mForeground  mode.   When this option is speci‚Äê[m
               fied, [1mssh-agent [22mwill not fork.[m
[m
       [1m-d      [22mDebug mode.  When this  option  is  specified,[m
               [1mssh-agent  [22mwill  not fork and will write debug[m
               information to standard error.[m
[m
       [1m-E [4m[22mfingerprint_hash[0m[m
               Specifies the hash algorithm  used  when  dis‚Äê[m
               playing  key fingerprints.  Valid options are:[m
               ‚Äúmd5‚Äù and ‚Äúsha256‚Äù.  The default is ‚Äúsha256‚Äù.[m
[m
       [1m-k      [22mKill  the  current   agent   (given   by   the[m
               SSH_AGENT_PID environment variable).[m
[m
       [1m-O [4m[22moption[0m[m
[7m Manual page ssh-agent(1) line 32 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K               Specify  an  option  when  starting [1mssh-agent[22m.[m
               Currently   two   options    are    supported:[m
               [1mallow-remote-pkcs11 [22mand [1mno-restrict-websafe[22m.[m
[m
               The  [1mallow-remote-pkcs11 [22moption allows clients[m
               of a forwarded [1mssh-agent [22mto  load  PKCS#11  or[m
               FIDO  provider libraries.  By default only lo‚Äê[m
               cal clients may perform this operation.   Note[m
               that  signalling  that  an [1mssh-agent [22mclient is[m
               remote is performed  by  [4mssh[24m(1),  and  use  of[m
               other  tools  to  forward  access to the agent[m
               socket may circumvent this restriction.[m
[m
               The   [1mno-restrict-websafe   [22moption   instructs[m
               [1mssh-agent [22mto permit signatures using FIDO keys[m
               that might be web authentication requests.  By[m
               default,  [1mssh-agent [22mrefuses signature requests[m
[7m Manual page ssh-agent(1) line 49 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K               for FIDO keys where the key application string[m
               does not start with ‚Äússh:‚Äù and when  the  data[m
               to  be  signed  does not appear to be a [4mssh[24m(1)[m
               user authentication request or a [4mssh-keygen[24m(1)[m
               signature.   The  default  behaviour  prevents[m
               forwarded  access  to a FIDO key from also im‚Äê[m
               plicitly forwarding the ability  to  authenti‚Äê[m
               cate to websites.[m
[m
       [1m-P [4m[22mallowed_providers[0m[m
               Specify a pattern-list of acceptable paths for[m
               PKCS#11  provider  and FIDO authenticator mid‚Äê[m
               dleware shared libraries that may be used with[m
               the [1m-S [22mor [1m-s [22moptions to [4mssh-add[24m(1).  Libraries[m
               that do not match the pattern list will be re‚Äê[m
               fused.  See PATTERNS in  [4mssh_config[24m(5)  for  a[m
               description  of  pattern-list syntax.  The de‚Äê[m
[7m Manual page ssh-agent(1) line 66 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K               fault list is ‚Äúusr/lib*/*,/usr/local/lib*/*‚Äù.[m
[m
       [1m-s      [22mGenerate  Bourne  shell  commands  on  stdout.[m
               This  is  the  default  if SHELL does not look[m
               like it's a csh style of shell.[m
[m
       [1m-t [4m[22mlife[0m[m
               Set a default value for the  maximum  lifetime[m
               of  identities  added to the agent.  The life‚Äê[m
               time may be specified in seconds or in a  time[m
               format  specified  in [4msshd_config[24m(5).  A life‚Äê[m
               time specified for an identity with [4mssh-add[24m(1)[m
               overrides this value.  Without this option the[m
               default maximum lifetime is forever.[m
[m
       [4mcommand[24m [[4marg[24m [4m...[24m][m
               If  a  command  (and  optional  arguments)  is[m
[7m Manual page ssh-agent(1) line 83 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K               given, this is executed as a subprocess of the[m
               agent.  The agent exits automatically when the[m
               command given on the command line terminates.[m
[m
       There  are  two main ways to get an agent set up.  The[m
       first is at the start of an X session, where all other[m
       windows or programs are started  as  children  of  the[m
       [1mssh-agent  [22mprogram.   The agent starts a command under[m
       which its environment variables are exported, for  ex‚Äê[m
       ample [1mssh-agent xterm &[22m.  When the command terminates,[m
       so does the agent.[m
[m
       The  second  method is used for a login session.  When[m
       [1mssh-agent [22mis started, it prints the shell commands re‚Äê[m
       quired to set its environment variables, which in turn[m
       can be evaluated in the  calling  shell,  for  example[m
       [1meval `ssh-agent -s`[22m.[m
[7m Manual page ssh-agent(1) line 100 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K[m
       In both cases, [4mssh[24m(1) looks at these environment vari‚Äê[m
       ables  and  uses them to establish a connection to the[m
       agent.[m
[m
       The agent initially does not have  any  private  keys.[m
       Keys  are  added  using  [4mssh-add[24m(1)  or by [4mssh[24m(1) when[m
       [1mAddKeysToAgent  [22mis  set  in  [4mssh_config[24m(5).   Multiple[m
       identities may be stored in [1mssh-agent [22mconcurrently and[m
       [4mssh[24m(1)   will   automatically  use  them  if  present.[m
       [4mssh-add[24m(1) is also used to remove keys from  [1mssh-agent[0m[m
       and to query the keys that are held in one.[m
[m
       Connections to [1mssh-agent [22mmay be forwarded from further[m
       remote  hosts  using  the [1m-A [22moption to [4mssh[24m(1) (but see[m
       the caveats documented therein), avoiding the need for[m
       authentication data to be stored  on  other  machines.[m
[7m Manual page ssh-agent(1) line 117 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K       Authentication  passphrases  and private keys never go[m
       over the network: the connection to the agent is  for‚Äê[m
       warded  over  SSH remote connections and the result is[m
       returned to the requester, allowing the user access to[m
       their identities anywhere in the network in  a  secure[m
       fashion.[m
[m
[1mENVIRONMENT[0m[m
       SSH_AGENT_PID  When  [1mssh-agent  [22mstarts,  it stores the[m
                      name of the agent's process ID (PID) in[m
                      this variable.[m
[m
       SSH_AUTH_SOCK  When [1mssh-agent  [22mstarts,  it  creates  a[m
                      Unix-domain socket and stores its path‚Äê[m
                      name  in this variable.  It is accessi‚Äê[m
                      ble only to the current  user,  but  is[m
                      easily  abused  by  root or another in‚Äê[m
[7m Manual page ssh-agent(1) line 134 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K                      stance of the same user.[m
[m
       In Debian, [1mssh-agent [22mis installed with the  set-group-[m
       id  bit  set,  to prevent [4mptrace[24m(2) attacks retrieving[m
       private key material.  This  has  the  side-effect  of[m
       causing the run-time linker to remove certain environ‚Äê[m
       ment  variables which might have security implications[m
       for    set-id    programs,    including    LD_PRELOAD,[m
       LD_LIBRARY_PATH,  and  TMPDIR.  If you need to set any[m
       of these environment variables, you will need to do so[m
       in the program executed by ssh-agent.[m
[m
[1mFILES[0m[m
       [4m$TMPDIR/ssh-XXXXXXXXXX/agent.<ppid>[0m[m
               Unix-domain sockets used to contain  the  con‚Äê[m
               nection  to  the  authentication agent.  These[m
               sockets should only be readable by the  owner.[m
[7m Manual page ssh-agent(1) line 151 (press h for help or q to quit)[27m[K[K               The  sockets  should get automatically removed[m
               when the agent exits.[m
